The seats will have less padding; passengers in these seats will be closer to the seat in front of them and behind them (less pitch), which affects legroom; and the seats do not recline (though Frontier calls them&#xA0;&#x201C;pre-reclined&#x201D;).&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ETo avoid all these pitfalls, a traveler would still have to purchase&#xA0;a middle seat in the more expensive premium economy &#x201C;Stretch&#x201D; section.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Fthe-new-airline-seat-that-turns-economy-into-business-101370413642.html\"\u003EThe New Airline Seat That Turns Economy Into Business Class\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EPerhaps the inch of extra room in the middle seat is to offset some of the other changes coming to Frontier. According to cntraveler.com, this year the airline is adding 12 seats to every Airbus A320 and A319 it flies. It&#x2019;s also set to be the first U.S. airline to put a 186-seat A320 into service, which has an extra six seats, thanks to smaller bathrooms.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EBut Frontier isn&#x2019;t worried about that:&#xA0;&quot;Customers fly on regional aircraft all the time when they can&#x2019;t stand up in the lavatory,&#x201C;says Daniel Shurz, chief commercial officer for Frontier. &quot;They handle that just fine.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EWATCH: Flying Singapore Airlines in First Class for an Hour Ruined My Life\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-embed tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Ciframe width=\"540\" height=\"303\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fscreen.yahoo.com\u002Fa-broad-abroad\u002Ffirst-class-broad-abroad-181008113.html?format=embed\"\u003E\u003C\u002Fiframe\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ELet Yahoo Travel inspire you every day. href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.sanparks.org\u002Fparks\u002Fkruger\u002F\"\u003EKruger National Park\u003C\u002Fa\u003E.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EIn the early hours of July 10, Carolyn Dunford was driving through the Orpen gate when she saw cars starting to slow down. That&#x2019;s when she noticed two huge male lions walking along the road, marking their territory.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EOut of nowhere, a large kudu bull appeared from the bushes. The first cat didn&#x2019;t seem too interested in the potential prey, but the second lion assumed the hunting stance and prepared to pounce.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"359\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F6ba8e56fd1125d467f9fa4c12239ae18ea972820.jpg\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EAs the kudu sprung into the road, the lion chased it down and attacked it right in front of the cars full of tourists. That&#x2019;s when the first lion got interested and came over to help.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Fback-from-extinction-lions-reintroduced-to-rwanda-123644475647.html\"\u003EBack From Extinction &#x2014;Lions Reintroduced to Rwanda\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;The other lion grabbed its throat and then there was no escape.&#x201D; Dunford wrote on \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fafricageographic.com\u002Fblog\u002Fkudu-killed-between-cars-in-kruger\u002F\"\u003EAfrica Geographic\u003C\u002Fa\u003E. &#x201C;The kudu died quickly and there was little struggle once both lions had it.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EAs the cars started to move away from the amazing scene, Dunford stayed behind.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"359\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F0379ed8415172b7ae3fd9991121bdb2228874bae.jpg\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;The males caught their breath and I was lucky to watch as the males began to feed,&#x201D; she wrote. &#x201C; They ate on the road for around half an hour before dragging the kudu off into the bushes to continue their meal.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EFew us will ever have the chance to see wild animals in nature, and for Dunford, it&#x2019;s a moment she&#x2019;ll never forget.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;An opportunistic hunt like this is a once in a lifetime sighting.&#x201D;\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EWATCH:&#xA0;A Visit with Baby Cheetahs in South Africa\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-embed tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Ciframe width=\"540\" height=\"303\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fscreen.yahoo.com\u002Fa-broad-abroad\u002Fvisit-baby-cheetahs-south-africa-173239889.html?format=embed\"\u003E\u003C\u002Fiframe\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ELet Yahoo Travel inspire you every day. Man Sets Appalachian Trail Record on 2,189-Mile Run","summary":"Scott Jurek, of Boulder, Colo., celebrates atop Mount Katahdin near Millinocket, Maine, after completing the Appalachian Trail in what he claims is record time.","body":"\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F8cb4dc2bf39f9e322f7ae59719b6673bb18ffc32.jpg\" alt=\"Colorado Man Sets Appalachian Trail Record on 2,189-Mile Run\" width=\"540\" height=\"714\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EScott Jurek, of Boulder, Colo., celebrates atop Mount Katahdin near Millinocket, Maine, after completing the Appalachian Trail in what he claims is record time. (Photo: AP)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EPORTLAND, Maine (AP)&#x2014; An ultramarathoner overcame an early injury, difficult terrain in New England and sleep deprivation on the final stretch of the Appalachian Trail to complete the trek in record time.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EDespite getting about 10 hours of sleep over the final four days, Colorado resident Scott Jurek reached the summit of Mount Katahdin on Sunday afternoon to finish the 2,189-mile run from Georgia to Maine in 46 days, eight hours. That bests the previous record held by Jennifer Pharr Davis by three hours.The 41-year-old Jurek nearly aborted the run in the mountains of Tennessee and North Carolina because of knee pain and a muscle tear that required him to walk for several days.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EBut he kept going.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;The biggest thing I&#x2019;m looking forward to is putting my feet up, being home and enjoying some downtime,&#x201D; he said Monday after getting his first seven-hour stretch of sleep since starting the run.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003ERelated:&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Fultimate-u-s-mountain-climbs-you-must-do-this-121771906692.html\"\u003EUltimate U.S. Mountain Climbs You Must Do This Summer\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EJurek, who has won several elite ultramarathon races, launched his extreme run May 27 at Springer Mountain, Georgia. His wife, Jenny, provided support for the run and joined him for the final race up Katahdin. Atop Maine&#x2019;s highest summit in Baxter State Park, about 200 miles from Portland, he kissed the mountaintop trail marker. Then he popped a bottle of Champagne, took a long swig and posed for pictures. He said it wasn&#x2019;t until the final stretch that he knew he&#x2019;d break the record.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"360\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F2d957f61a0738cb4bcb1d67dfe3bf37ac008d50b.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EJurek, winner of several ultramarathon races, began at Springer Mountain in northern Georgia on May 27. (Photo: AP)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EDavis, the previous record holder, tweeted her congratulations with a photo showing her hoisting a beer in his honor. His finish represents the fastest known time, but no organization tracks or verifies trail records. &#x201C;Everything is based on the honor system,&#x201D; said Javier Folgar from the Appalachian Trail Conservancy in Harpers Ferry, West Virginia.The trail is a difficult challenge. Hiking it means climbing more than 30 peaks, wading several dozen streams and rivers, and enduring the famed &#x201C;100-mile wilderness.&#x201D; And that&#x2019;s only for the segment in Maine. The trail passes through 13 other states.Only about one in four of the estimated 2,500 to 3,000 people who start the hike actually finish the trek.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Fdeadliest-sport-ever-why-people-risk-their-lives-87909897077.html\"\u003EDeadliest Sport Ever? Why People Risk Their Lives Mountain Climbing\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;Every individual hikes the Appalachian Trail for their own personal reason and their own personal goals. It goes along with the saying, &#x2018;Hike your own hike,&#x2019;&#x201D; Folgar said. &#x201C;We&#x2019;d like to congratulate Scott and all other thru-hikers and section hikers and other folks who attempted to hike the Appalachian Trail.&quot;Jurek said his days as a competitive runner are numbered and he viewed this endurance run as his &quot;masterpiece&#x201D; before starting a family with his wife. In the end, he said, it didn&#x2019;t go exactly as he planned because he had to try to make up for lost time at the end. But he said he had no regrets about doing something he&#x2019;d never tried before.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EHe said everyone should push themselves, whether it&#x2019;s hiking or other activities.&#x201C;That&#x2019;s what makes it a true adventure. It was about pushing my body mentally and physica! lly but also going into that unknown space,&#x201D; he said. &#x201C;Anybody can do that. It may not be on the Appalachian Trail or running a marathon. It&#x2019;s putting yourself in a situation that&#x2019;s a challenge to find that source of strength that you didn&#x2019;t think you had.&#x201D;\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EWATCH:&#xA0;Wipeout! Burkard&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Cspan\u003EWhy:\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cspan\u003E&nbsp;Of all the city streets I have traveled, none rival Ocean Road in Havana, Cuba. It is literally the epicenter for life in the country, the crossroad for locals, tourists and vendors. I walked around for hours with my camera, often before the sunrise and all the way till sunset. Axelrod\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Cspan\u003EWhy:\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cspan\u003E Carrera 7 is one of the main avenues that crosses Bogota, and holds a lot of historical importance. It runs through La Candelaria, the first neighborhood of Bogota and Plaza de Bolivar, were this image was taken. In the background is the Cathedral of Bogota. The avenue is always very visual, with pop-up vendors, and the bustle of a capitals main through fare. Here a young girl with her Llama, which is used to attract tourist who can pose for photographs with the animal. There is always something to photograph on the street and down its picturesque side alleys.\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\u003Cb\u003EAbout Nicolas:\u003C\u002Fb\u003E \u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\u003C\u002Fspan\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cspan\u003EBogota, Colombia is coming into its own as a travel destination once more. There&#x2019;s nothing like floating on a lake on your back or in a boat. It&#x2019;s old-fashioned family fun. Actually, it&#x2019;s just plain fun for everyone. Try some of these most-searched lake vacations on Yahoo. Formed over 7,000 years ago by the collapse of a volcano, the lake is nearly 2,000 feet deep. Perhaps the most unique thing about it is that the lake isn&#x2019;t fed by any rivers or streams. Instead, through evaporation and rain\u002Fsnowfall, the water is completely replaced about every 250 years. In the summer, you can swim, fish, or boat. Just be warned: it&#x2019;ll probably be cold. By mid-July, Rim Drive is also open so you could try biking, hiking, or driving all the way around the breathtaking and historic lake.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E9. \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fsearch.yahoo.com\u002Fsearch?p=Table+Rock+Lake+Hotels&amp;pvid=_VOvHTIwOC7VCUNrUuhGJgtMMjA5LlMORjv_1b2I&amp;fr=trvl_mktg_content&amp;.tsrc=trvl_mktg_content&amp;pn=yahoo_mobile_us_web&amp;type=-list_US_Lakes&amp;soc_src=mail&amp;soc_trk=ma\"\u003ETable Rock Lake\u003C\u002Fa\u003E: Family-Themed Fun\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"304\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F420675fdbd680614d7afe92e7d55aec2269302df.jpg\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003ETable Rock Lake. (Photo:&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.flickr.com\u002Fphotos\u002Fmuffintoptn\u002F\" title=\"Go to John Starnes&apos;s photostream\"\u003EJohn Starnes\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u002FFlickr)\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003ESure, maybe you visit Branson, Mo., for the 1800s-themed amusement park, live music, and Dolly Parton&#x2019;s Wild West dinner theater. But, while you&#x2019;re there, you might want to check out Table Rock Lake. The lake sits just outside of town, in the Ozarks, and was created by a dam built in the 1950s. On the east side, \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fmostateparks.com\u002Fpark\u002Ftable-rock-state-park\"\u003ETable Rock State Park\u003C\u002Fa\u003E has boating, swimming, and camping for visitors.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003ERelated:&#xA0; \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Fbest-lake-beaches-in-america-89975847942.html\"\u003EYou Don&#x2019;t Need an Ocean with These Best Lake Beaches in America\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E \u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E8. \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fsearch.yahoo.com\u002Fsearch?p=Caddo+Lake&amp;pvid=_VOvHTIwOC7VCUNrUuhGJgtMMjA5LlMORjv_1b2I&amp;fr=trvl_mktg_content&amp;.tsrc=trvl_mktg_content&amp;pn=yahoo_mobile_us_web&amp;type=-list_US_Lakes&amp;soc_src=mail&amp;soc_trk=ma\"\u003ECaddo Lake\u003C\u002Fa\u003E: Under the Cypress Trees\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EOn the border of Louisiana and and Texas, Caddo Lake is a protected wetlands and home to the largest cypress forest in the world, and it&#x2019;s a beautiful spot to canoe through lush vegetation. It is also the site of several&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Ftexaslesstraveled.com\u002Fbigfootcountry.htm\"\u003EBigfoot sightings\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, so keep your eyes peeled. Stay in one of \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Ftpwd.texas.gov\u002Fstate-parks\u002Fcaddo-lake\u002Ffees-facilities\u002Fcabins\"\u003Ethe popular cabins in Caddo Lake State Park\u003C\u002Fa\u003E and explore the maze of bayous and ponds that make up the lake. (Or \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.caddolakecabins.com\u002F\"\u003Erent a private cabin\u003C\u002Fa\u003E.) But beware of alligators, which frequent the park and lake. You might want to read \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Ftpwd.texas.gov\u002Fstate-parks\u002Fpark-information\u002Falligator-safety\u002Falligator-safety\"\u003Ethese alligator safety tips\u003C\u002Fa\u003E before hitting the water.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E7. \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fsearch.yahoo.com\u002Fsearch?p=Lake+Powell&amp;pvid=_VOvHTIwOC7VCUNrUuhGJgtMMjA5LlMORjv_1b2I&amp;fr=trvl_mktg_content&amp;.tsrc=trvl_mktg_content&amp;pn=yahoo_mobile_us_web&amp;type=-list_US_Lakes&amp;soc_src=mail&amp;soc_trk=ma\"\u003ELake Powell\u003C\u002Fa\u003E: Lounging on the Lake\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"359\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fefd9c3f9079687faaeeca2799e9e439d9ba7d241.jpg\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003ELake Powell. (Photo: Wikimedia Commons)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003ENearly 2 million people each year visit Lake Powell, on the border of Utah and Arizona. It was originally created by the Glen Canyon Dam, which filled Glen Canyon with water. It&#x2019;s now the second largest man-made reservoir in the country. The lake, a popular destination in the summer, sits next to the \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.nps.gov\u002Fglca\u002Findex.htm\"\u003EGlen Canyon National Recreation Area\u003C\u002Fa\u003E. While you can explore the Orange Cliffs and larger park, most visitors simply rent a houseboat and lounge on the water. There are five marinas &#x2014; four with launch ramps. With almost 2,000 miles of shoreline, Lake Powell is an ideal spot for a family vacation or a fun get-together with friends.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E6. \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fsearch.yahoo.com\u002Fsearch?p=Lake+Shasta&amp;pvid=_VOvHTIwOC7VCUNrUuhGJgtMMjA5LlMORjv_1b2I&amp;fr=trvl_mktg_content&amp;.tsrc=trvl_mktg_content&amp;pn=yahoo_mobile_us_web&amp;type=-list_US_Lakes&amp;soc_src=mail&amp;soc_trk=ma\"\u003ELake Shasta\u003C\u002Fa\u003E: At the Mountain&#x2019;s Base\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"270\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F761e32e0209dfcbb156d6f85a2ff6726634ceebf.jpg\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003ELake Shasta. (Photo:&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.flickr.com\u002Fphotos\u002Fpsyberartist\u002F\" title=\"Go to psyberartist&apos;s photostream\"\u003Epsyberartist\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u002FFlickr)\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003ELake Shasta, in Northern California, is popular for its clear water and stunning views of Mt. Shasta. Covering nearly 30,000 acres across its surface, the lake has more than enough room for boating, fishing, and water-skiing. Bridge Bay is the largest marina, known for \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.bridgebayhouseboats.com\u002F\"\u003Eits houseboat rentals\u003C\u002Fa\u003E and lodge right on the water. A warning, though: With the drought in California, the water in Lake Shasta is low. Check the conditions before you go &#x2014; though it could also mean some cheap deals as the crowds stay away. Or you could use it as an opportunity to visit the nearby \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Flakeshastacaverns.com\u002F\"\u003ELake Shasta Caverns\u003C\u002Fa\u003E and possibly catch a glimpse of the submerged towns and tunnels under the lake.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E5. \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fsearch.yahoo.com\u002Fsearch?p=Lake+Ozarks&amp;pvid=_VOvHTIwOC7VCUNrUuhGJgtMMjA5LlMORjv_1b2I&amp;fr=trvl_mktg_content&amp;.tsrc=trvl_mktg_content&amp;pn=yahoo_mobile_us_web&amp;type=-list_US_Lakes\"\u003ELake of the Ozarks\u003C\u002Fa\u003E: Miles and Miles of Magic\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EAlso known as &#x201C;The Magic Dragon,&#x201D; the Lake of the Ozarks in Missouri could more accurately be described as a kind of large, twisting river. Because of its winding shape, the lake is over 90 miles long and has over 1,100 miles of shoreline to explore and visit. Originally constructed to provide hydroelectric power to state residents, it has become a major tourist attraction and resort area. Over 5 million people visit the lake annually. Because it&#x2019;s so large, there are a number of different things to do: golf, relax, or party on the water. \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fmostateparks.com\u002Fpark\u002Flake-ozarks-state-park\"\u003ELake of the Ozarks State Park\u003C\u002Fa\u003E is also home to Party Cove (formally known as Anderson Hollow Cove), which is exactly what it sounds like.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated:&#xA0; \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Fbest-lake-vacations-in-the-c1407188808446.html\"\u003ELake Vacations in the U.S. That Have Everyone Reaching for Their Swimwear\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E \u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E4. \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fsearch.yahoo.com\u002Fsearch?p=Lake+Havasu&amp;pvid=_VOvHTIwOC7VCUNrUuhGJgtMMjA5LlMORjv_1b2I&amp;fr=trvl_mktg_content&amp;.tsrc=trvl_mktg_content&amp;pn=yahoo_mobile_us_web&amp;type=-list_US_Lakes&amp;soc_src=mail&amp;soc_trk=ma\"\u003ELake Havasu\u003C\u002Fa\u003E: A Party on the Water\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"541\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F42e1202f541c04344749f28e71251023f98a79f7.jpg\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003ESpring breakers tubing on Lake Havasu. (Photo:&#xA0;jessica.vanni\u002FTwenty20)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EA popular spot for college spring breakers and people looking to let loose, Lake Havasu is known as a floating party. But the large reservoir on the border of Arizona and California is also a beautiful natural playground. If you get tired of boating, fishing, and floating, check out the \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.fws.gov\u002Frefuge\u002Fhavasu\u002F\"\u003EHavasu National Wildlife Refuge\u003C\u002Fa\u003E upriver from the lake, the \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.fws.gov\u002Frefuge\u002Fbill_williams_river\u002F\"\u003EBill Williams River National Wildlife Refuge\u003C\u002Fa\u003E downriver, or \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fazstateparks.com\u002FParks\u002FLAHA\u002F\"\u003ELake Havasu State Park\u003C\u002Fa\u003E on the eastern shore. Stay in Lake Havasu City and don&#x2019;t forget to visit the London Bridge &#x2014; a bridge that originally was built across the Thames River in England until it was dismantled and moved to Arizona.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E3. \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fsearch.yahoo.com\u002Fsearch?p=Big+Bear+Lake&amp;pvid=_VOvHTIwOC7VCUNrUuhGJgtMMjA5LlMORjv_1b2I&amp;fr=trvl_mktg_content&amp;.tsrc=trvl_mktg_content&amp;pn=yahoo_mobile_us_web&amp;type=-list_US_Lakes&amp;soc_src=mail&amp;soc_trk=ma\"\u003EBig Bear Lake\u003C\u002Fa\u003E: Among the Mountains\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"810\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F5d64012040f82fee913b0a7611427528a17ba9ff.jpg\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EBig Bear Lake. (Photo:&#xA0;Shestock \u002F Alamy)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EUp in the mountains about two hours east of Los Angeles, Big Bear Lake is both the name of a lake and the small town next to it, which is a heavily visited ski destination in the winter. But in the summer, the seven-mile lake welcomes vacationers looking to fish, boat, or hike. While the town has a permanent population of just over 5,000, on popular weekends it can house as many as 100,000 people. Sitting near the San Bernardino National Forest, the area is known for its amazing views and miles of trails.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E2. \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fsearch.yahoo.com\u002Fsearch?p=Lake+Champlain&amp;pvid=_VOvHTIwOC7VCUNrUuhGJgtMMjA5LlMORjv_1b2I&amp;fr=trvl_mktg_content&amp;.tsrc=trvl_mktg_content&amp;pn=yahoo_mobile_us_web&amp;type=-list_US_Lakes&amp;soc_src=mail&amp;soc_trk=ma\"\u003ELake Champlain\u003C\u002Fa\u003E: Quiet Island Paradise\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"677\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F0fb8c7ece68b871a0c89362803d6a61dc6f1d167.jpg\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EBurlington Breakwater South Lighthouse on Lake Champlain. (Photo:&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.flickr.com\u002Fphotos\u002Ftonythemisfit\u002F\" title=\"Go to Tony Fischer&apos;s photostream\"\u003ETony Fischer\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u002FFlickr)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003ENear the Canada border, Lake Champlain is a freshwater lake in the valley between the Adirondack Mountains and the Green Mountains. The lake contains nearly 80 islands, including the large islands of South Hero and North Hero, which are home to some year-round residents in addition to summer vacationers. Take a \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.ferries.com\u002F\"\u003Eferry\u003C\u002Fa\u003E to get around and be sure to visit the historic lighthouses that dot the islands. While the lake and its islands are known for their natural beauty and quiet seclusion &#x2014; particularly in spots like \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.vtstateparks.com\u002Fhtm\u002Fsandbar.htm\"\u003ESand Bar State Park\u003C\u002Fa\u003E in Vermont and \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fparks.ny.gov\u002Fparks\u002F30\u002Fdetails.aspx\"\u003EPoint Au Roche State Park\u003C\u002Fa\u003E on the New York side, you can also enjoy the non-natural wonders, like \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.lakechamplainchocolates.com\u002F\"\u003ELake Champlain chocolates\u003C\u002Fa\u003E.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated:&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Fcycling-around-lake-tahoe-americas-best-bike-ride-100013929797.html\"\u003ECycling Lake Tahoe: Crazy Inclines, Bears, and Even a Casino Pit Stop\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E \u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E1. \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fsearch.yahoo.com\u002Fsearch?p=Lake+Tahoe&amp;pvid=_VOvHTIwOC7VCUNrUuhGJgtMMjA5LlMORjv_1b2I&amp;fr=trvl_mktg_content&amp;.tsrc=trvl_mktg_content&amp;pn=yahoo_mobile_us_web&amp;type=-list_US_Lakes&amp;soc_src=mail&amp;soc_trk=ma\"\u003ELake Tahoe\u003C\u002Fa\u003E: Skiing or Swimming\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"360\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F1166017234a652a184d6a345fa62096618b26055.jpg\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003ELake Tahoe. (Photo: Thinkstock)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EAt 1,600 feet deep and just over 70 miles around, Lake Tahoe, Calif., is one of the largest and deepest lakes in the country. It&#x2019;s also one of the prettiest. Sitting at 6,000 feet elevation and surrounded by mountains, which house nearly a dozen large and popular ski resorts in the winter, Lake Tahoe is known for its clear and crisp water. Often divided into areas referred to as the North Shore and the South Shore, Lake Tahoe is home to countless small towns, secluded beaches, and mountainous hiking trails (and on the Nevada side, casinos). Check out Emerald Bay or mountain bike the famous Flume Trail. For the more adventurous, the Tahoe Rim Trail makes a 165-mile loop around the lake.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E WATCH: \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Flets-get-one-thing-straight-i-am-not-a-seafaring-111502312517.html\"\u003EDid Sinbad Get This Seasick? Hitting the High Seas of Oman \u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-embed tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Ciframe width=\"540\" height=\"303\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fscreen.yahoo.com\u002Fa-broad-abroad\u002Flife-dhow-fisherman-broad-abroad-205000730.html?format=embed\"\u003E\u003C\u002Fiframe\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E \u003Cb\u003ELet Yahoo Travel inspire you every day. Lee\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIf throwing yourself into a volcano as a sacrifice to the gods is not on the top of your adventure to-do list, there are plenty of other ways to get your volcanic\u003Ci\u003E&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fi\u003Ethrills on. From sandboarding down an active volcano in Nicaragua to dangling over hot lava in Chile, here some of the coolest eruptive excursions from around the world: \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E1.\u003C\u002Fb\u003E \u003Cb\u003EVolcano Surfing,&#xA0;\u003Cb\u003ECerro Negro, Nicaragua\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F07e60fab4b1501046d0b4e1d442becb683685642.jpg\" alt=\"These Volcano Adventures Around the World Will Blow Your Mind\" width=\"540\" height=\"540\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EVolcano surfing. (Photo: Lanee Lee)&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;Lean back and let it rip!&#x201D; shouted Miguel Garcia, my \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fcoxandkingsusa.com\"\u003ECox &amp; Kings\u003C\u002Fa\u003E&#xA0;&#x201C;surfing&#x201D; instructor. Suddenly, I was zooming down Cerro Negro&#x2019;s ash slope on a narrow wooden board as black pebbles pelted my face. Twenty seconds later, I reached the bottom of the hill, limbs still intact. Although I didn&#x2019;t break the 95-kilometer-per-hour (about 59 mph) speed record, it felt like I had. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Ftierratour.com\u002Ftours\u002F15.html\"\u003ECerro Negro\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, located roughly an hour outside of Leon, Chile, is the world&#x2019;s only active volcano that you can board down, be it sitting or standing. Due to the volcano&#x2019;s remote location, it&#x2019;s best to opt for a guided trek. Outfitters provide an English-speaking hiking guide, boards, and safety equipment, such as the (prison-style) jumpsuit, goggles, and gloves.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002F10-reasons-to-go-to-nicaragua-now-102292614864.html\"\u003E10 Reasons to Go to Nicaragua Now\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E 2. Volcano Camping,&#xA0;\u003Cb\u003EAcatenango, Guatemala\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"356\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Ff8f66f0e766d61e0ff94424842bf5b6a236e659e.png\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EPhoto: Guatemala Tourism board\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ETake sleeping in the elements to a whole new level with \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fadventureguatemala.com\u002Facatenango-volcano\u002F\"\u003EAdventure Guatemala&#x2019;s\u003C\u002Fa\u003E two-day trek and camping excursion. Summit Acatenango volcano by day; watch \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fovfuego-norte.geo.mtu.edu\u002F\"\u003EFuego\u003C\u002Fa\u003E&#xA0;&#x2014;&#xA0;the world&#xED;s most consistently erupting volcano &#x2014; spew its angry fire and fumes by night, while camping on a nearby crater\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E3. \u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cb\u003ELava Boating,&#xA0;\u003Cb\u003EMt. Kilauea, Hawaii&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"359\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fc5f03f401f83df0f16a4527aaa47ff0a1a0a97fe.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EPhoto: Lava Ocean Tours\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EContinually erupting since 1952, Kilauea is aptly named &#x2014; it means &#x201C;spewing&#x201D; in Hawaiian. Since you can no longer do a \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.nautilusdivehilo.com\u002Findex.php?option=com_content&amp;view=article&amp;id=92&amp;Itemid=160\"\u003Ehot-lava scuba dive\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, the next best adrenaline rush is to feel the heat under your feet on a guided hike on Kilauea&#x2019;s lava fields, followed by a boat tour to witness the fiery show of red, liquid rock meeting the ocean in a steamy billow of clouds. Hot tip: Because volcanic activity changes daily, check the state&#x2019;s daily Kilauea \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fhvo.wr.usgs.gov\u002Factivity\u002Fkilaueastatus.php\"\u003EVolcano Update\u003C\u002Fa\u003E or \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.seelava.com\u002Flavacombo\u002F\"\u003ELava Ocean Tours\u003C\u002Fa\u003E to make sure lava is flowing into the ocean before booking.&#xA0; \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Flife-lessons-i-learned-on-the-road-to-hana-109589923237.html\"\u003ELife Lessons from Maui: What I Learned Driving the Crazy Road to Hana\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E4. Snowboarding,&#xA0;Mount Ruapehu, New Zealand\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-embed tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Ciframe height=\"404\" width=\"540\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.youtube.com\u002Fembed\u002Fh8W_sGYAQlc?feature=oembed&amp;start=122\"\u003E\u003C\u002Fiframe\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.mtruapehu.com\u002F\"\u003EMount Ruapehu\u003C\u002Fa\u003E has two of the largest ski fields in New Zealand. Nothing too crazy about that, right? Well, it&#x2019;s also the country&#x2019;s most active volcano. (The last eruption was in 2007.) Of course, plenty of safety precautions are in place in case of an eruption, such as an alarm that sounds alerting you to head to higher ground to avoid lahars (rivers of volcanic mud). Nothing like running from lava to spice up your snowboard or ski vacation. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E5. \u003Cb\u003EBungee Jumping,&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fb\u003EVillarrica Volcano, Chile\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-embed tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Ciframe height=\"404\" width=\"540\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.youtube.com\u002Fembed\u002Fp9wqouoFAX4?feature=oembed\"\u003E\u003C\u002Fiframe\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EVideo: Youtube\u002F\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.youtube.com\u002Fchannel\u002FUCqfchntZr4pm-Hz6g8hgpTQ\"\u003EDesignTendencia\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EPerhaps you&#x2019;ve bungee jumped from a bridge or platform, but how about from a helicopter? Perched on the helicopter&#x2019;s skid, you leap from 10,000 feet in the air, heading straight for a molten pool of lava. Luckily, the cord yanks you back 700 feet above Vllarrica&#x2019;s caldera. Then you&#x2019;re transported back to the airport dangling upside down from the helicopter, roughly 35 minutes away. Run by \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.bungee.com\u002Fbzapp\u002Fvolcano\u002F\"\u003EBungee\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, the jump is part of a five-day adventure. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E6. \u003Cb\u003EVolcano Cable Car,&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fb\u003EThrihnukagigur, Iceland\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"347\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F5ebc59634d8c2edd3394fef04bff75b86b1ad477.png\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EPhoto: Extreme Iceland\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EEyjafjallajokull is Iceland&#x2019;s most infamous volcano thanks to its show-stopping (and flight-halting) antics in 2010. However, there is only one way you can actually descend into its belly. The 4,000-year dormant Thrihnukagigur reveals its secrets only to those who venture in by way of a cable car. Go down 400 feet into one of its magma chambers for views of Mother Nature&#x2019;s art &#x2014; a spectrum of rainbow-colored residue on the rock walls. Day trips by \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.insidethevolcano.com\"\u003EInside the Volcano\u003C\u002Fa\u003E run May through September. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E7. \u003Cb\u003EHorseback Riding\u002FJeeping,&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fb\u003EMount Bromo, Indonesia\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"351\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Ffea49ee63924c2dfe2b14a9af59d4d8d11415fd0.png\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EPhoto: Wonderful Indonesia\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;Bound by wild desire, I fell into a ring of fire,&#x201D; Johnny Cash once crooned. Indonesia&#x2019;s Ring of Fire, a string of volcanoes along the basin of the Pacific Ocean, has a similar effect &#x2014; especially in\u003Ca\u003E Bromo Tengger Semeru National Park\u003C\u002Fa\u003E. Start in the wee hours of the morning with a bumpy off-road jeep ride, followed by a stunning sunrise hike to Mount Bromo&#x2019;s smoking volcano crater, or head out on a horseback ride across a desert of ash. See it on your own or go with a tour operator, such as \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fbromosunrisetour.com\u002F\"\u003EBromo Sunrise Tour\u003C\u002Fa\u003E.&#xA0; \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E8. \u003Cb\u003EVolcano Biking,&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fb\u003ECotopaxi, Ecuador\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"360\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F724cdd464b2d49ebf6991bd180cd78d91df57a76.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EPhoto: Steve Ogle\u002FAdventure Life\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.volcano.si.edu\u002Fvolcano.cfm?vn=352050\"\u003ECotopaxi\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, located roughly 38 miles from Quito,&#xA0;has been silent for almost 75 years. However, it&#x2019;s starting to \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.wired.com\u002F2015\u002F06\u002Frestless-volcano-puts-ecuador-edge\u002F\"\u003Erumble once again\u003C\u002Fa\u003E. Before it decides to blow its top, head out on a four-day mountain biking trek with \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.adventure-life.com\u002Ftours\u002Fcotopaxi-mountain-biking-3951\"\u003EAdventure Life\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, cycling through Santa Rita Ecological Reserve, El Tambo Trail, The Road of the Lahars, and down the volcano itself. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Fgalapagos-island-volcano-erupts-first-time-in-33-119938416827.html\"\u003EGalapagos Island Volcano Erupts for First Time in 33 Years\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E9. \u003Cb\u003EHeli-Skiing,&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fb\u003EKamchatka Peninsula\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cb\u003E, Russia&#xA0;\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"360\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fbdc88fd7f367c8a7d536de13e7ee14bf82020eb8.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EPhoto: 56th Parallel\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EOn this eight-day excursion exploring Russia&#x2019;s Far East volcanic slopes with \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.56thparallel.com\u002Frussia-tours\u002Fkamchatka-heli-skiing-russia\u002F\"\u003E56\u003Csup\u003Eth\u003C\u002Fsup\u003E Parallel\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, it&#x2019;s possible to ski on five different volcanoes and even into craters with active steam vents. Optional volcanic thrills include snowmobiling, dogsledding, and geothermal hot springs.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E10. \u003Cb\u003EZip-Lining,&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fb\u003EArenal, Costa Rica\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"383\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fa77c61edd90d0a9d3b60428e19bbfd50f8cdd968.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EPhoto: Sky Trek\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EArenal is just one of six active volcanoes in Costa Rica, albeit, the most-visited of them all. And it&#x2019;s also one of the best spots to zip-line with epic volcano vistas. The two-and-a-half hour tour with \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fskyadventures.travel\u002Fskytrek\u002F\"\u003ESky Trek\u003C\u002Fa\u003E begins with a gondola ride to the top of the trees. From there, you&#x2019;ll fly through the air on seven cables, with volcano and lake views, at an elevation of roughly 2,500 feet.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E11. \u003Cb\u003EGeothermal Cooking,&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fb\u003EMount\u003C\u002Fb\u003E \u003Cb\u003ETavurvur, Papua New Guinea\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"419\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F43a2b62e7ada2bf34c1421bbed729001efc2fe70.png\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EPhoto: PNG Tourism\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIf all these extreme volcano adventures, aren&#x2019;t enough, there&#x2019;s always the novelty of cooking your breakfast via one. Local birds &#x2014; called megapodes &#x2014; lay eggs in the volcanic ash at the hot springs near Tavurvur volcano in Indonesia. As part of a six-hour guided hike to the volcano&#x2019;s peak with \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.diveandtoursrabaul.com\u002Ftours#.VZWFoufSg1I\"\u003EDive and Tours\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, you&#x2019;ll learn to do what the locals do: spot the nests, gather the eggs, and then boil them in the hot springs. Hot tip: Don&#x2019;t try this hike without a guide. Local villagers own sections of the volcano and you need special permits to pass. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EWATCH: The Blue Lagoon: Geothermal Spa Heaven&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-embed tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Ciframe width=\"540\" height=\"303\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fscreen.yahoo.com\u002Fa-broad-abroad\u002Fblue-lagoon-geothermal-spa-heaven-070000315.html?format=embed\"\u003E\u003C\u002Fiframe\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ELet Yahoo Travel inspire you every day. Surfing, and Sasa  8 Reasons to Go to Samoa Now!","summary":"While Samoa has long been a beach-flop destination for a few New Zealanders and Australians, it doesnt register that high on the international radar. Here are some of the highlights on the island ofSavaii.","body":"\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F19159a1c137f1c2539756da239e774a441722301.jpg\" alt=\"Sun, Surfing, and Sasa &#x2014; 8 Reasons to Go to Samoa Now!\" width=\"540\" height=\"428\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThere are few places left in the world that can actually be considered exotic. The independent country of \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.samoa.travel\u002F\"\u003ESamoa\u003C\u002Fa\u003E&#x2014;formerly known as Western Samoa and not to be confused American Samoa&#x2014;is one of them. The tiny archipelago is far from anywhere in the South Pacific, and is a place of sugar-soft beaches, people dressed in sarongs (called lava lavas here), intriguing traditional dances, and little evidence that this is the 21\u003Csup\u003Est\u003C\u002Fsup\u003E century. Still, it&#x2019;s safe, welcoming, and ultimately not all that hard to get to (a 5.5-hour flight from Honolulu or 3.5 hours from Auckland).\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EBut the best part is that there&#x2019;s no one else there&#x2014;yet.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EWhile Samoa has long been a beach-flop destination for a few New Zealanders and Australians, it doesn&#x2019;t register that high on the international radar. However, word is getting out and American brands are starting to setting up shop. There are two new Sheraton Resorts in the capital and near the international airport, and a few new smaller establishments.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EEven with the growth, it&#x2019;s common to have one of those white beaches all to yourself. That&#x2019;s especially true on Savai&#x2019;i, the less populated of the two main islands, with just 42,000 people on about 650 square miles, and no big resorts. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EHere are some of the highlights on&#xA0;Savai&#x2019;i.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EThe Alofaaga Blowholes\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"321\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fcc245cc6b36016f9f1a2a02bc968af0f1d734252.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EWhen my Facebook status mentioned Samoa, friends started asking if I&#x2019;d seen the blow holes yet. It&#x2019;s rare that people get so uniformly excited about a geological feature, but this one is seriously crazy. \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.samoa.travel\u002Factivity\u002Falofaaga-blowholes\"\u003EThe Alofaaga Blowholes\u003C\u002Fa\u003E are a series of gaps in the volcanic rocks along the coast of Savai&#x2019;i that allow waves to come in, before forcing them violently 100 feet into the air. Buy some coconuts from the local vendors, toss them in at the right moment, and watch them fly!\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003ERelated:&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Fdaydream-sua-ocean-trench-upolu-island-samoa-122786327287.html\"\u003E#Daydream: Sua Ocean Trench, Upolu Island, Samoa\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EThe dances\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"359\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fcca05740d0056f283e0c1988af3255aafb957a67.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EForget any hula shows you may have seen in Hawaii or cultural performances in Tahiti. If you see dancing here, it&#x2019;s because it&#x2019;s really time to dance &#x2014; with or without tourists in the audience.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThe most common dances are a lively male counterpart to the hula called the sasa, and the slightly violent fa&#x2019;ataupati, or &#x201C;slap dance,&#x201D; in which men slap their bodies in ways said to have been derived from the motions of killing insects. And then there&#x2019;s the taualuga, in which a group of men dance around a woman, then lie down in turns so she can step on their backs.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EThe surf is out of this world\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"318\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Ffa77cc9158bec62fd0bb59efda69e3c729d20560.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EAside from the Kiwi beach-floppers, the main group of people who have typically visited Samoa have been serious surfers. They love the bragging rights associated with surfing gnarly waves&#x2014;and the area is full of them. But it&#x2019;s not just for super advanced surfers &#x2014; even brand-new beginners can enjoy. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EThere&#x2019;s a terrific new lodge\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"360\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fd4bed76b326af425f577b81bc985136db25e1dcf.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EMainly marketed as a surf destination, the new \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fpegasuslodges.com\u002Faganoa-lodge\u002F\"\u003EAganoa Lodge Samoa\u003C\u002Fa\u003E is much more than that. Sure, the spectacular point break is just a short swim from the main house, but it&#x2019;s hardly the only reason to visit. Reopened after a major investment from a group of Americans in February, the lodge consists of eight dreamy open-air fales, whose beds are mere steps from the beach. Beyond surfing, Aganoa offers SUP, snorkeling, island sightseeing, and simply relaxing on the empty white beach. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EAfu Afu Falls\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"317\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F389ff0df4acf59ce83d817731f26ea026581bcb6.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ESamoa is hot&#x2014;the average temperature is 86F, and the water is 77F. The cold-water showers at many of the fale accommodations (including Aganoa) come as a relief. Looking for an even better way to cool off? Take a five-minute hike followed by a leap of a rock edge into the cool freshwater pool beneath the \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.samoa.travel\u002Factivity\u002Fafu-aau-falls\"\u003EAfu Afu Falls.\u003C\u002Fa\u003E It&#x2019;s a short swim across to the base of the falls, where you can pose for a terrific photo.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003ERelated:&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Ftop-10-islands-in-the-world-81317893291.html\"\u003ETop 10 Islands in the World\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EFabulous churches\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"359\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F45249092e9642cf800d1a0ac894c3c5b3cf9e44b.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ERegardless of your religious beliefs, it&#x2019;s worth going to church on a Sunday to see Samoan culture at its most distinctive and vibrant. The 19\u003Csup\u003Eth\u003C\u002Fsup\u003E-century missionaries were effective, and the overlay of Christianity on the traditional culture is fascinating. You see it whenever you drive by a brightly colored church, whose over-the-top architectural style you can&#x2019;t quite name. There&#x2019;s a nightly evening prayer curfew around 6 p.m.&#x2014;which can be annoying, as visitors aren&#x2019;t supposed to drive during that time. But nothing but church happens on Sundays anyway, so you might as well go. Everyone in the villages turns out in their best clothes for an hour of exuberant singing and celebration.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EThere&#x2019;s no Starbucks\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"390\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F792189689894ddd3ee4597a11e391db1dd0390ef.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EOr any other sign of Western culture. There&#x2019;s little need for caffeine anyway, as life moves awfully slow here. A market sells skip-able souvenirs (lava lavas, wood carvings, shell jewelry), there&#x2019;s a decent local beer (which tastes pretty much like any other tropical-island beer) and an ice cream shop with interesting tropical fruit flavors. But really, you don&#x2019;t even need them. The best thing to eat is fish, especially the just-caught sashimi that&#x2019;s served nightly as an appetizer at Aganoa. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003EWATCH: Wipeout! Surfing With Famed Chef Eric Ripert in Puerto Rico. Not as Easy as It Looks\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-embed tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Ciframe width=\"540\" height=\"303\" allowfullscreen data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fscreen.yahoo.com\u002Fa-broad-abroad\u002Fsurfing-eric-ripert-broad-abroad-070000528.html?format=embed\"\u003E\u003C\u002Fiframe\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ELet Yahoo Travel inspire you every day. to Eat Asian Street Food and Not Get Sick","summary":"Asian street food has a reputation for making foreigners sick. Here's how to eat great food safely.","body":"\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EB\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.fivedollartraveller.com\u002F\"\u003Ey Meagen Collins and Tom Williams\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EAsian street food has a reputation for making foreigners sick. After 14 months of travel in Asia and only a couple of instances of mild diarrhea, we&#x2019;ve maintained a pretty solid system (pun) for avoiding getting sick from eating street food.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EWe&#x2019;d like to share our top tips with you.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EOne of the major ways we keep our budget down while travelling Asia is by eating street food. On the street you can get a tasty meal for less than a dollar in many countries &#x2014; while the restaurants are charging up to $5 or more.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EWe understand that by western standards, getting a full restaurant meal for $5 is a sweet deal, and the fear of getting &#x201C;Delhi Belly&#x201D; or any other nasty gastro (we have all heard the nasty poop stories) is a real concern.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EBut if you want to save money, eat incredible food, and get more of an authentic experience by eating what the locals eat, then pay attention to the following tips about the best ways to find tasty treats that won&#x2019;t upset your stomach or your wallet.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F09623b9315c84fd37366041a1829d18b4622086b.png\" alt=\"How to Eat Asian Street Food and Not Get Sick\" width=\"540\" height=\"360\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EStreet vendors have ways of keeping their food bacteria-free. (All photos: Meagen Collins and Tom Williams)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E1. Making people vomit is bad for business\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIt is death for any business, be it a street vendor or a Michelin star restaurant, for ANY of their patrons to get sick. If they are providing food, they will &#x201C;try&#x201D; to make things as safe as possible. Otherwise they no longer have an income. Which in Asian countries can mean extreme poverty.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003ERelated:&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Fstreet-snacks-around-the-world-89376653272.html\"\u003EThe Tastiest Street Snacks Around the World\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ESome places have little tricks to make food safer. We read that the reason you may find street curries very oily is because this top layer of oil acts to guard off bacteria from the meats in the curry below. The process is similar to preserving other types of food in jars. These methods protect the food and make it better for us, the consumer. &#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E2. Eat where the locals eat\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIf you pass by a street vendor that has no local customers, this is usually for a reason. Source out the food you&#x2019;re interested in trying and then see how many locals are also digging in. This is often a great way to find the best food in town, and sometimes the best price too.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"480\" height=\"640\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w480\u002Fed6e24abe0ba8fdfcca9eef876cc528f301c8ab9.png\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E3. Are they cooking fresh?\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThere a quite a few street stalls that will cook early in the morning and then sell their food throughout the day. In places with higher temperatures this can be asking for trouble, especially if meat is involved! Feel free to indulge first thing in the morning, but as the day gets warmer give these places a miss.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated:&#xA0; \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Fwhere-to-get-asian-street-foods-117185413562.html\"\u003EThe Most Mouth-Watering Street Foods in Asia\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThe best places are the ones where you can see they are continuously cooking. You can also ask for food to be reheated, rather than just picking some half-cold item straight off the cart.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E4. There&#x2019;s something in the water\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ECalling it &#x201C;food&#x201D; poisoning can be a misnomer. Often it&#x2019;s water poisoning. Floating fecal matter (yes, microbe sized bits of poo) in untreated water gets on your food, your toothbrush, and many other places if you don&#x2019;t pay attention to when tap water is used. Diseases like typhoid are regularly transmitted this way.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThorough cooking often kills that sort of bacteria. So the big pile of deep fried chicken may actually be healthier than a raw green salad that was rinsed before serving.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EAvoid anything that is uncooked, as well as anything with ice cubes that weren&#x2019;t made with drinking water.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E5. Beware of the fruit. That rhyme about an apple a day doesn&#x2019;t always work\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EMany vendors will sell various melons already cut up, and on a hot day this may look very appetizing, but \u003Cb\u003Edo not eat\u003C\u002Fb\u003E the sliced fruit! Most of the time it has been out all day being attacked by flies, dust, and who knows what else. Sometimes the vendor may spray the melon with water to make it look fresher, so the nasty water you have just been trying to avoid is all over your fruit.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EWhich brings me to my second point on this: rinse your fruit in bottled water. Just as you would do at home to get rid of any lingering pesticides, it&#x2019;s best to do the same here.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EOur suggestion is to stick to bananas or unopened fruit. Most vendors will open up a fresh papaya or mango and cut it up for you on the spot.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"360\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fc04f012d46ad6e0e05bf07528a5363e195ff3d3d.png\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E6. Does it look safe to try, and how many flies can you count?\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Col\u003E\n \u003Cli\u003EIs the food kept covered or out in the open?\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n \u003Cli\u003EIs raw meat \u002F seafood kept on ice?\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n \u003Cli\u003EHow recently was the dish you wanted cooked?\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n \u003Cli\u003EAre they making an effort to keep the flies away?\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n \u003Cli\u003EHow clean does the stall, equipment, and cook look&#x2026;..we are serious about the cook, these countries don&#x2019;t use plastic gloves, so their hands in and all over your food.\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\u003C\u002Fol\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E7. Is now the time to change to the other side&#x2026; become vegetarian?\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EOne reason many people get sick is from bad meat, so we ask the question&#x2026;: do you really need meat in every dish?\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ESome countries such as India have amazing vegetarian options available where many travelers have said they don&#x2019;t even miss meat.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ETip: In some Asian countries such as Vietnam, they do still consider &#x201C;vegetarian&#x201D; to include pork. We found the best way around this is to ask for &#x201C;monks food&#x201D; as buddhist monks are strict vegetarians and locals seem to have a better concept of this than some tourist trying to explain that pork broth is still pork.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"360\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F6bc97d28c030f3fcd410dec61e811f083f0a0acc.png\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E8. Clean your hands\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EFrom working on cruise ships, we learned early on that it&#x2019;s not always dodgy preparation of food that makes people sick. It&#x2019;s all the filth \u003Ci\u003Eyou \u003C\u002Fi\u003Eare carrying around on your hands.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EMum had it right when she made you wash your hands before dinner. Do the same here and wash them thoroughly or sanitize with baby wipes or antibacterial soap before putting your fingers anywhere near your food or mouth.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated:&#xA0; \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Fthe-best-street-foods-in-trinidad-121601439127.html\"\u003EThe Best Street Foods in Trinidad\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIf you are in a country where the tap water is unsafe for consumption, an alcohol-based hand sanitizer is a much better option than rinsing your hands in typhoid water.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E9. What would Oprah do&#x2026; follow your gut instinct!\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIf you bite into something that &#x201C;just doesn&#x2019;t seem right,&#x201D; don&#x2019;t just assume that&#x2019;s how it&#x2019;s meant to taste. Sometimes is best to err on the side of caution and leave the rest of the meal in the bin.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"360\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fc71805820dec54cf765b8f1386ad621f3cdb4de4.png\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EBonus tip: get a better-priced meal\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EOK, so this has nothing to do with eating street food and not getting sick, but the financial benefits to eating street food are huge.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EIt is sometimes possible to haggle to get a better price, especially if there are no written prices. If you feel you a getting ripped off and being charged &#x201C;tourist prices,&#x201D; you can move onto the next vendor selling the same dish and see if you can get a better deal.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"405\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fd99ee9c20f0daacfa074bb64148af11eb8c48ce6.png\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EA dollar here and there can make a BIG difference while travelling!\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EBottom line: don&#x2019;t be afraid to try new foods on the street. There are an amazing assortment of tasty treats waiting for you outside of that cushy overpriced restaurant that is selling you the same &#x201C;chicken and rice&#x201D; meal every night.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ESo get out there give it a go, eat some crazy thing on a stick though you&#x2019;re not entirely certain what it is, and enjoy the world of street food!\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EWATCH: \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Fspend-the-best-day-of-your-life-in-an-elephant-102339382037.html\"\u003ESpend the Best Day of Your Life in an Elephant Retirement Home \u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-embed tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Ciframe width=\"540\" height=\"303\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fscreen.yahoo.com\u002Fa-broad-abroad\u002Fbroad-abroad-elephants-212200811.html?format=embed\"\u003E\u003C\u002Fiframe\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E \u003Cb\u003ELet Yahoo Travel inspire you every day. Years Old and 30 Countries Down  Meet the Worlds Youngest Travel Blogger","summary":"Tatum Oxenreider is just ten years old but she has already traveled to more than 30 countries. Now she has your dream job.","body":"\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F1c608fb5b689ee3e3caf5214eb1a51d4e56d62a6.jpg\" alt=\"10 Years Old and 30 Countries Down &#x2014; Meet the World&#x2019;s Youngest Travel Blogger\" width=\"540\" height=\"306\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003ESnorkeling in the Great Barrier Reef, Queensland, Australia. (Photo: Tsh OxenReider)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EWhat&#x2019;s better than traveling the world, experiencing one-of-a-kind adventures, and then getting paid to write about them? &#xA0;Being a travel writer is a highly coveted job that many writers dream of landing one day.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThe position is typically reserved for those with a pedigree of published pieces and thousands of miles under their belts, so the thought of a kid taking on that role seems relatively impossible. That&#x2019;s until \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Ftheartofsimpletravel.net\u002Fauthor\u002Ftatum\u002F\"\u003ETatum Oxenreider \u003C\u002Fa\u003Eentered the picture.\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fyhoo.it\u002F1GuXBRu\"\u003EEverything You Need to Know to Be a Travel Blogger\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EAt 10 years old, she&#x2019;s been to over 30 countries and has spent most of her life on the road with her parents, who work for a nonprofit and run their company \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Ftheartofsimpletravel.net\u002Fabout\u002F\"\u003EThe Art of Simple Travel\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, and two brothers. School days are spent visiting places like the Eiffel Tower or the Great Wall of China instead of sitting in a classroom. Her parents have been encouraging her to write about her experiences as part of her untraditional lesson plan. &#x201C;I enjoy writing because I can just let my ideas out on a piece of paper; then others can read about them and know about them,&#x201D; Tatum tells Yahoo Travel.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"405\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F32d998429d295efb5988522da1fcfc3d84820ffa.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EThe family of five in China. (Photo: Tsh Oxenreider)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ETatum&#x2019;s mom Tsh was the first one to encourage her daughter to start blogging. She began taking the next steps of teaching her daughter how to turn those writings into publishable pieces. &#x201C;We were already having her keep a journal of the places we&#x2019;ve gone to,&#x201D; Tsh tells Yahoo Travel. &#xA0;&quot;So, we thought we could turn this into more of a lesson by polishing them up and posting them online, and it would be great for people to get a kid&#x2019;s perspective of traveling and the benefits of it.&#x201C;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ENow, Tatum contributes to her mom&#x2019;s successful travel blog \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Ftheartofsimpletravel.net\u002Fabout\u002F\"\u003EThe Art of Simple Travel\u003C\u002Fa\u003E and has written pieces such as &quot;My Day at Elephant Nature Park&#x201D; and &#x201C;Queensland, Australia is Awesome for Kids.&#x201D; Her charming posts are part humor, part photos, and part tour guide, just what you&#x2019;d expect from any seasoned writer.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fyhoo.it\u002F18iqTqP\"\u003EA Teen Travel Blogger on What It&#x2019;s Like to Travel the World\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThe burgeoning blogger was even approached by HomeAway to write about how long-term travel has changed her life. &#x201C;Not only is long-term travel brain-changing and fun, but it is also life-changing,&#x201D; she wrote in the piece. &#xA0;&quot;I have most definitely grown, not only in height and muscles, but my heart as well. I have really matured.&#x201C; It&#x2019;s that viewpoint that her mother says makes her feel like it&#x2019;s all worth it. &quot;Of course, they&#x2019;re kids and they complain and whine when we&#x2019;re on the road,&#x201D; says Tsh. &#x201C;But, getting to read everything she&#x2019;s taking away from our travels makes us feel like we&#x2019;re doing something right.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"360\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F9c8b89dad19dd3c9b83c479acd2138a2f59c89ed.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003ETatum feeding the elephants in&#xA0;Chiang Mai, Thailand. (Photo: Tsh Oxenreider)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ETatum hopes her writing and blogging will help change the idea that it is hard to travel with kids. &#x201C;I want people to learn that what you dream about is possible if you just believe it can happen,&#x201D; she adds. &#x201C;Put action behind your travel dreams, and it really can happen. We&#x2019;re a very normal family, and we did it!&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fyhoo.it\u002F1GMbUkL\"\u003ETravel the World for Free &#x2014; Become a Luxury Travel Advisor\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003ESo, could full-time travel writing be something that runs in the family? &#x201C;I want to be a biologist when I grow up,&#x201D; says Tatum. &#x201C;But, I could also be a blogger and just write about biology.&#x201D;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003ELet Yahoo Travel inspire you every day. Well, that is a whole different story.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThat&#x2019;s why we love the trend of wedding registries that allow you to customize a honeymoon experience and then ask your guests to pay for it. (Photo: Wanderable)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EWanderable&#x2019;s co-founders, Jenny Chen and Marcela Miyazawa, first came up with the idea for the site when Miyazawa was researching honeymoon registries for her own wedding. She was frustrated with the market &#x2014; the companies that she tested all had poor design and unintuitive user flows.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fyhoo.it\u002F1Humtrs\"\u003EConfessions of a Las Vegas Wedding Chapel Officiant\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;We have always wanted to be an easy and inspiring alternative for couples who already have all the household things they need and want to register for amazing honeymoon experiences instead,&#x201C;&#xA0;Miyazawa said.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EWanderable allows customers to quickly create a free and beautiful online honeymoon registry, which they can personalize with their own fonts, colors, and photos. You can browse&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.wanderable.com\u002Fdestinations\"\u003Ecurated experiences\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, but couples can also add anything else they wish to their registry.&#xA0;\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"428\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F79e780015151e29e08160e0555efefd5e4e6cb1e.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EThe site works with hotels from the Shangri-La in Paris to the Four Seasons in Florence. (Photo: Wanderable)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EOnce their registry is completed, the couple shares it with their wedding guests. Wedding guests can then make online purchases toward the couple&#x2019;s registry. Couples receive automatic notifications from Wanderable for all gifts received. Depending on which type of gift it is, they will either receive cash which will be deposited directly into their bank account or the travel item will be booked directly through a vendor.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"325\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002Fa669024343ac99dfdfe47b825173a15213d79f51.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EYou don&#x2019;t just have to register for high-end fancy things. Use the registry to get delicious dumplings. Post-Breakup Road Trips to Get Your Mojo Back","summary":"If your relationship has tanked, set your GPS for one of these epic post-breakup road-trip locations.","body":"\u003Cfigure
