\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EBy Meghan Rabbit\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EAfter a relationship has tanked to the point of no return, there&#x2019;s nothing quite like getting in the car &#x2014; either by yourself or with a bestie or two &#x2014; and taking your mind off everything on the open road. So queue up Tom Petty&#x2019;s &#x201C;Free Falling&#x201D; and set the GPS for one of these epic post-breakup road trips.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003EYour post-breakup mood:\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cb\u003E &#x201C;Bring on the vino.&#x201D;\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Ci\u003EWhere to go: \u003C\u002Fi\u003EThe Finger Lakes, N.Y.\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"485\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F90d9b77ab193437ca8cb4d3c6b02c8582121dc40.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EExcelsior Glen Falls in Watkins Glen of the Finger Lakes. (Photo:&#xA0; \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.flickr.com\u002Fphotos\u002Fshobeir\u002F\" title=\"Go to Shobeir Ansari&apos;s photostream\"\u003EShobeir Ansari\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u002FFlickr)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThe scenic drive on routes 5 and 20 in the \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.fingerlakestravelny.com\u002F\"\u003EFinger Lakes region\u003C\u002Fa\u003E of central New York offers a 135-mile &#x201C;corridor&#x201D; that crosses a ton of lakeside hotspots. Start in Ithaca and make a day trip to Cayuga Lake for a \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.winolimo.com\"\u003EWater to Wine Tour\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, which&#xA0;lets you cruise from winery to winery by boat. When you&#x2019;re back in town, soak up some of that vino at \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.moosewoodcooks.com\u002F\"\u003EMoosewood Restaurant\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, the iconic vegetarian eatery that&#x2019;s said to be one of the inspirations of the plant-based movement in the &#x2019;70s. The next day, head to the heart of the Finger Lakes Wine Trail for lunch at \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.flxwienery.com\u002F\"\u003EF.L.X. Weinery\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, a casual spot where all the locals go for an array of gourmet hot dogs, hamburgers, sausages, and French fries. Don&#x2019;t miss tastings at \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.glenora.com\u002F\"\u003EGlenora Wine Cellars\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.foxrunvineyards.com\u002F\"\u003EFox Run Vineyards\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, and \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.belhurst.com\"\u003EBelhurst Estate Winery\u003C\u002Fa\u003E.&#xA0;When you&#x2019;re wine-d out, check out the oil and vinegar tasting at \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.folivers.com\"\u003EF. Oliver&#x2019;s\u003C\u002Fa\u003E (the squash seed and grapeseed oils are musts), or take a stand-up paddleboard \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.tuneyoga.com\"\u003E(SUP) yoga class\u003C\u002Fa\u003E on Canandaigua Lake.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003ERelated:&#xA0; \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Fthe-perfect-luxurious-weekend-in-california-wine-120150050312.html\"\u003EA Luxurious Road Trip Through California&#x2019;s Wine Country\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003EYour post-breakup mood: \u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cb\u003E&#x201C;Flirting my way back into the game.&#x201D;\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Ci\u003EWhere to go:\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E \u003Cb\u003EColorado\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"360\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F7637e272410001ac7a6108247d6cc3d453b7b691.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EA rainbow tableau in Breckenridge. (Photo:&#xA0;\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.flickr.com\u002Fphotos\u002F20980483@N04\u002F\" title=\"Go to Ed Ogle&apos;s photostream\"\u003EEd Ogle\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u002FFlickr)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThere&#x2019;s something about mountain towns that inspire serious flirtation. Maybe it&#x2019;s the adrenaline pumping through your body after an epic run down a mountain trail on skis, a snowboard, or a bike. Or maybe it&#x2019;s the fact that, for those interested in the male species, Colorado&#x2019;s male-to-female ratio is very much in your favor. (Denver got its nickname &#x2014; &#x201C;Menver&#x201D; &#x2014; for good reason, after all!)\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EStart in Denver and drive to Breckenridge for great food, plenty of microbreweries, and the opportunity to participate in every mountain sport ever created. From there, continue west along I-70, taking in stunning mountain vistas until you reach Glenwood Springs. After a soak in the healing waters at the \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.hotspringspool.com\"\u003EGlenwood Hot Springs Lodge\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, drive over Independence Pass to Aspen. (Note: Don&#x2019;t attempt this during the snowy winter months, when the road closes, because it&#x2019;s too treacherous to travel &#x2014;&#xA0;and skip this hairpin-turns-everywhere road if you get carsick.)\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated:&#xA0; \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Fjust-dumped-adventures-beyond-kilimanjaro-119937468709.html\"\u003EJust Dumped? Adventures to Take Beyond Kilimanjaro\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EYou&#x2019;ll find more great food and bars in high-end Aspen, plus luxe accommodations at reasonable prices at \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.theskyhotel.com\u002F?&amp;utm_source=Google%20My%20Business&amp;utm_medium=GMB&amp;utm_campaign=GMB&amp;utm_term=sky\"\u003EThe Sky Hotel\u003C\u002Fa\u003E. Into the great outdoors? Hike the Maroon Bells from Aspen to Crested Butte, a stunning 12-mile walk through wildflower-filled trails with epic views. Rather road trip? Take the 100-mile spectacularly beautiful drive over the Elk mountains to the Butte for &#x2014; you guessed it &#x2014; even \u003Ci\u003Emore\u003C\u002Fi\u003E great food, brews, and a laid-back mountain town vibe.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003EYour post-breakup mood:\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cb\u003E &#x201C;Take me to a spa &#x2014; stat.&#x201D;\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Ci\u003EWhere to go:\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Ci\u003E \u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003Cb\u003EArizona\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"285\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F323aabe85729fb1d39470efed62b773457fc5a0e.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003EWell &amp; Being Spa at the Fairmont Scottsdale Princess. (Courtesy: Fairmont)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EYes, it&#x2019;s home to the country&#x2019;s retired snowbirds during winter as well as Major League Baseball training camps in early spring, but Arizona is&#xA0;also a veritable mecca of world-class spas. To wit: The mac daddies of all spas &#x2014; Canyon Ranch and Miraval &#x2014; are located in Tucson and will both make you feel so blissful that you&#x2019;ll never want to leave. In addition to a little pampering at the spas across the state, there are plenty of other attractions to inspire you when you decide to swap that terry cloth robe for real clothes.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EStart in Tucson at \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.ritzcarlton.com\u002Fen\u002FProperties\u002FDoveMountain\u002FSpa\u002FDefault.htm\"\u003EThe Ritz Carlton Spa Dove Mountain\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, where you&#x2019;ll find eco-holistic treatments based on the traditions of the Sonoran Desert. From the Desert Gemstone Ritual in which you allow your spirit to choose a&#xA0;stone that calls to you, to the Hohokam Stone Massage based on Native American traditions, there are many options that&#x2019;ll help heal a broken heart. From here, skip the freeway and take the scenic routes 77, 79 and 60 to Scottsdale, making a beeline for the \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.fairmont.com\u002Fscottsdale\u002Fspa\u002F\"\u003EWell &amp; Being Spa\u003C\u002Fa\u003E at the Fairmont Scottsdale Princess. After spending a few minutes in their waterfall tub you&#x2019;ll feel like any leftover &#x201C;gunk&#x201D; from your breakup wash away.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EWhen you&#x2019;re feeling refreshed, hit the road again and take routes 87 and 260 to Sedona, where there are powerful energy vortexes beneath the red rock landscape &#x2014; swirling centers of energy that are reportedly conducive to spiritual healing, meditation, and self-exploration. Stay at \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fmiiamo.com\"\u003EMii Amo\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, voted one of the world&#x2019;s best destination spas, which offers customized, all-inclusive packages that include treatments, fitness and nutrition counseling, spiritual practices, and pretty much everything else you can think of that&#x2019;ll help heal your heartbreak.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003EYour post-breakup mood:\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003Cb\u003E &#x201C;It&#x2019;s my breakup and I&#x2019;ll cry if I want to.&#x201D;\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Ci\u003EWhere to go:\u003C\u002Fi\u003E Nevada\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"348\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F7cdfd3aca5a1e77a7f05b147ae14e52fb2022be0.jpg\"\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003ELonely Highway 50. (Photo: Ron Reiring)\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThe Nevada desert mountains and empty road of Highway 50 is the perfect place to get some headspace and let your emotions flow. After all, it&#x2019;s home to&#xA0;what \u003Ci\u003ELife\u003C\u002Fi\u003E magazine coined the \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fyhoo.it\u002F1v95mpn\"\u003ELoneliest Road in America\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, thanks to its hauntingly beautiful landscapes and very little traffic &#x2014; you can go 20 miles or more without seeing another car. That means it&#x2019;s the perfect place to sob as you listen to old Alanis Morissette albums. Nobody will hear you.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003EThis road starts in Fernley, near the California border, and stretches 287 miles to Ely, near the Utah border. Make your first stop in \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.visitfallonnevada.com\u002F\"\u003EFallon\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, an old cowboy town that was home to the real Navy base featured&#xA0;in the film \u003Ci\u003ETop Gun\u003C\u002Fi\u003E. From there, hit \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.austinnevada.com\"\u003EAustin\u003C\u002Fa\u003E&#xA0;to watch or try world-class landsailing &#x2014;&#xA0;just like normal&#xA0;sailing, except you sit in a three-wheeled go cart-like vehicle instead of a boat &#x2014; or soak in the nearby hot springs. If you&#x2019;re feeling a little down, stay in the old mining town of \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.co.eureka.nv.us\"\u003EEureka\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, right in the heart of Highway 50 and known as the Friendliest Town on the Loneliest Road in America. Stay here at \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.eurekagoldcountryinn.com\u002Fjackson_house_hotel.html\"\u003EThe Jackson Hotel\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, built in 1877, then celebrate the fact that you survived this old Pony Express in \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.elynevada.net\"\u003EEly\u003C\u002Fa\u003E at Great Basin National Park, where you can go spelunking in Lehman Caves, fishing on Baker Creek, or hike the 13,063-foot Wheeler Peak (the second highest peak in Nevada).\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EMore from ShermansTravel:\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fblog.shermanstravel.com\u002F2015\u002F5-of-hawaiis-most-beautiful-waterfalls\u002F\"\u003EHawaii&#x2019;s Most Beautiful Waterfalls\u003C\u002Fa\u003E \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fblog.shermanstravel.com\u002F2015\u002Fwhere-to-go-in-august-2015\u002F\"\u003EBest Places to Go in August for Adventure, Spa-ing, and More\u003C\u002Fa\u003E \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fblog.shermanstravel.com\u002F2015\u002F5-yoga-retreats-you-wont-want-to-sneak-out-of\u002F\"\u003E5 Yoga Retreats You Won&#x2019;t Want to Sneak Out Of\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003EWATCH:&#xA0; Meet Candace: The Woman Who Cross Dressed Her Way Through Afghanistan \u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-embed tmblr-full\"\u003E\n \u003Ciframe width=\"540\" height=\"303\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fscreen.yahoo.com\u002Fa-broad-abroad\u002Fmeet-candace-woman-cross-dressed-173200589.html?format=embed\"\u003E\u003C\u002Fiframe\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\u003Cp\u003E \u003Cb\u003E\u003Cb\u003ELet Yahoo Travel inspire you every day. Greenlands Finest Microbrew Beers","summary":"I'm a beer woman. So on my trip to Greenland, when I heard there was a craft brewery in town, I made a beeline for it.","body":"\u003Cp\u003EAnybody who knows me knows I don&#x2019;t drink vodka. I don&#x2019;t do tequila. And I&#x2019;ve never been a big fan of anything that comes with a garnish. I am, however, a beer girl. Raised in Cincinnati, a town with German roots, I have a deep love of hops, and over the years my tastes have been refined from \u003Ca href=\"http:\u002F\u002Fhudepohlbeer.com\u002F\"\u003EHudepohl\u003C\u002Fa\u003E and Schlitz to craft beers. Don&#x2019;t get me wrong &#x2014; when stuck on a riverboat for a bachelorette party in, say, Austin, Texas (thanks to my sister Emily), I will still happily down a Bud, a Coors, or a Schlitz. But I have learned to appreciate the fine craft of beer making and love a small-batch brew. So on my trip to Greenland, when I heard there was a craft brewery in town, I made a beeline for it.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cb\u003E\u003Ci\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Ffinger-pulling-head-pulling-and-kick-the-seal-122521580652.html\"\u003EFinger Pulling and Kick the Seal &#x2014; Welcome to the Arctic Games!\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F93fb6d09ed4cf36c50b1cd8100b9a9da95be5f9d.png\" alt=\"Taste-Testing Greenland&#x2019;s Finest Microbrew Beers\" width=\"540\" height=\"304\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EThe Godthaab Bryghus brewery is in a building that conveniently also houses a dive bar called Daddy&#x2019;s. While &#x201C;Daddy&#x201D; is a great guy named Gert, the actual brewery is run by Mikael Sorenson, who swears that the beer there is made with glacier ice that is at least 2,000 years old.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E&#x201C;Yes, we have men who go out onto the ice and cut slabs off the glaciers for us and bring them back here for our beer,&#x201D; Sorenson said.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E[Side note: Apparently ice cutting is a big business. Down the street is an ice cream shop that also uses 2,000-year-old ice. &#x201C;Ice cream in Greenland?&#x201D; you may be asking. &#x201C;Isn&#x2019;t it cold enough?&#x201D; No. It&#x2019;s not. Greenland has the second largest ice cream consumption per capita in the world, second only to Finland. Go figure.]\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cfigure class=\"tmblr-full\"\u003E \n \u003Cimg src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fg\u002Fimages\u002Fspaceball.gif\" alt=\"image\" width=\"540\" height=\"304\" data-src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fs.yimg.com\u002Fcd\u002Fresizer\u002F2.0\u002FFIT_TO_WIDTH-w540\u002F3a590de53797cb2f646953e3212a190735cb2dff.png\"\u003E \n\u003C\u002Ffigure\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EWhile there are no official stats on how much beer is consumed in &#xA0;Nuuk, Greenland&#x2019;s capital, judging by the crowds in the bars and the continual snow, I&#x2019;d say it ranks right up there. And frankly, I can&#x2019;t say I blame them &#x2014; the weather is rough (see previous episode: &#x201C;\u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Fsnowmageddon-2015-cabin-fever-hits-hard-in-123462240287.html\"\u003ESnowmageddon 2015: Cabin Fever Hits Hard in Greenland\u003C\u002Fa\u003E&#x201D;), and the beer is delicious. At the time I visited, there were five beers on tap, including the Musk Ox, the Eric the Red, and the Polar Bear (they like to name the beers after local animals). And here&#x2019;s a tip: While they are all delicious, if you ever find yourself at Daddy&#x2019;s in Nuuk, ask for Gert and Mikael and get them to give you the unfiltered versions of all the beers. They may smell like dirty feet, but they taste like heaven.&#xA0;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Ci\u003E\u003Cb\u003ERelated: \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.yahoo.com\u002Ftravel\u002Fsnowmageddon-2015-cabin-fever-hits-hard-in-123462240287.html\"\u003ESnowmageddon 2015: Cabin Fever Hits Hard in Greenland\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fi\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E \n\u003Cp\u003EThere is only one problem with the Godthaab Bryghus beer &#x2014; while it is possibly the best beer I have ever tasted (and trust: I have tasted a lot of beer), they don&#x2019;t export. So to get 2,000-year-old glacier-water beer, you have to go to the source. It&#x2019;s worth it. \u003Cbr\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\u003Cb\u003ELet Yahoo Travel inspire you every day.
